Status: `0x0036` is not only a death/retreat test. It is a generic actor property predicate. Retreat/death labels map cleanly to current-HP-zero tests; actor selector namespaces remain undecidable. Property `15` is exact at byte level (`HistoryActor+0xfc`) and likely image/appearance-related from native loader evidence, but it is not exercised by current script records and should not be mapped as status/ailment.

### 4.10 `DecodeScenes` Flow-Control Runtime Evidence

`ScriptHandler::DecodeScenes@0x00708abd` is the remaining structural gate for a safe dumper. It does not just walk a flat record list; it builds per-section script lists, tracks child/subscript depth, and treats raw commands `0x0000..0x0007` specially before or after normal `Script*::initPara`.

Header and section evidence:

| Native address | Instruction hex | Decoded instruction | Runtime meaning |
|---:|---|---|---|
| `0x00708b60`-`0x00708b74` | `0a 21`; `bl bytesToInt`; `subs #0xa`; `asrs #2` | read `bytesToInt(buf,0x0a)` and compute `(headerSize-0x0a)/4` | Confirms section count comes from the header-size table. |
| `0x00708bdc`-`0x00708be8` | `lsls section,#2`; `adds #0xa`; `bl bytesToInt` | read section offset at `0x0a + section*4` | First section offset is included in the table. |
| `0x00708bea`-`0x00708bfa` | `bl bytesToShort`; `adds r5,#2` | read section script-count, then advance past it | Each section begins with a short count. |
| `0x00708c0a`-`0x00708c18` | allocator + memset | allocate a per-section count/index table | The decoder records how many physical records belong to each logical subblock. |

Raw `cmd <= 7` jump table:

The Thumb switch helper at `0x00708c5e` reads eight bytes starting at `0x00708c62`:

```text
04 10 17 2c 2c 2c 2c 1c
```

Using the Thumb table rule `target = 0x00708c62 + tableByte * 2`, the targets are:

| Raw cmd | Native class / role | Target | Runtime effect |
|---:|---|---:|---|
| `0x0000` | base `Script(0)` structural marker | `0x00708c6a` | If the `ScriptChildInfo` skip flag is set, clear it, advance by one extra short, and continue; otherwise decrement logical nesting depth before normal base-script handling. |
| `0x0001` | base `Script(1)` structural marker | `0x00708c82` | Set child/subscript mode, increment logical nesting depth, then continue through normal handling. |
| `0x0002` | `ScriptChildInfo` | `0x00708c90` | If not already in child/subscript mode, set the next-zero skip flag; otherwise keep child/subscript mode. Then parse normally. |
| `0x0003` | `ScriptElse` | `0x00708cba` | Normal virtual `initPara` / append-or-execute path. |
| `0x0004` | `ScriptTestAsk` | `0x00708cba` | Normal virtual path. |
| `0x0005` | `ScriptTestValue` | `0x00708cba` | Normal virtual path. |
| `0x0006` | `ScriptForceLimit` | `0x00708cba` | Normal virtual path. |
| `0x0007` | `ScriptTestStartBattle` | `0x00708c9a` | Special start-battle/list selection path, then normal virtual path when applicable. |

Base/default script evidence:

| Native address | Instruction hex | Decoded instruction | Runtime meaning |
|---:|---|---|---|
| `0x006fed38` | `81 80` | `strh r1,[script,#4]` | `Script::Script(int)` preserves the raw command id in object field `#4`. |
| `0x006fecac` | `10 1c` | `adds r0,r2,#0` | Base `Script::initPara` consumes no payload and returns the incoming payload offset. |
| `0x006fecb4`-`0x006fecbc` | `ldrsh [script,#4]`; `bl DMemoryWriter::writeShort` | Base `Script::saveScript` writes only the raw command short. |
| `0x006fecd0`-`0x006fecf4` | read `#4`, compare `0/1`, adjust global test index | Base `Script::HandleScript` makes raw `cmd 0/1` affect the global condition stack. |

`ScriptTestStartBattle` (`cmd 0x0007`) itself has no extra payload:

- `ScriptTestStartBattle::saveScript@0x00709f55` is the base pattern: read `#4`, write one short.
- `ScriptTestStartBattle::HandleRScript@0x00709f45` reads `RedeScreen#0x2c`, subtracts `9`, and returns a test-style result for the current R-screen battle-start state.
- Therefore the `DecodeScenes` special path for raw `cmd 7` is list/section selection around a payloadless command, not hidden binary parameters.

Append/execute path:

| Native address | Instruction hex | Decoded instruction | Runtime meaning |
|---:|---|---|---|
| `0x00708cc0`-`0x00708cca` | load vtable slot `#8`; `blx` | call `Script*::initPara(buf,payloadOffset)` | Every command-specific parser advances the byte offset. |
| `0x00708e16`-`0x00708e22` | `bl Script::setSubScript`; `bl DList<Script>::addElement` | set subscript id, append script to current list | Load/list mode keeps scripts as executable objects instead of immediately executing them. |
| `0x00708e2c`-`0x00708e3c` | compare cmd `0x004b`; virtual call slot `#0x18` | immediate `HandleScript` path, except `ScriptDispatchOwn` | Non-list mode can execute records while decoding; `0x004b` is intentionally not executed there. |
| `0x00708e3e`-`0x00708e58` | increment current count; if nesting depth zero, store count in table | close one logical subblock | The per-section count table later drives list/sublist reconstruction. |
| `0x00708e76`-`0x00708f4c` | allocate `DList<Script>`, copy ranges based on the count table, add to handler list | materialize nested script lists | Physical records become grouped logical script lists after the first pass. |

Special non-flow-control side effects inside decode:

| Native address | Instruction hex | Decoded instruction | Runtime meaning |
|---:|---|---|---|
| `0x00708d14`-`0x00708d2e` | compare cmd `0x0027`; load `#0x32`; write handler `#0x0c` | `ScriptMoneyTest` stores a replay/branch index-like value | Important for exact replay/branch state; not yet mapped to CCZ. |
| `0x00708d30`-`0x00708d74` | compare cmd `0x0077`; call `ScriptValueOperation::getNum2` | selected `ScriptValueOperation` records update local decode variables | These values later affect deployment handling. |
| `0x00708d76`-`0x00708d98` | compare cmd `0x004b`; adjust `#0x24` by `local*16` | `ScriptDispatchOwn` list index may be adjusted by previous value ops | Player deployment decoding must emulate this, not parse `#0x24` in isolation. |

Status: the flow-control byte shape is no longer opaque, but the flat `prefix + cmd` simplification was wrong. A safe dumper must emulate raw `cmd 0/1/2/7` structural behavior, switch between subblock-start `prefix + cmd` records and in-subblock `cmd`-only records, call each `initPara`, apply child/subscript extra-short skips, and reconstruct logical script lists from the count table. What remains unknown is the exact high-level meaning of some handler/global fields, the complete runtime meaning of `ScriptTestStartBattle` list selection, and the choice-branch subblock transition around `ScriptShowChoice`.

### 4.11 Native-Mode Parser Corrections

This pass corrected the first corpus-dumper failure by tracing `R_01.eex_new` section `0x001e` against `DecodeScenes` and native `initPara` routines. The failing bytes were not encrypted or text-corrupt; the parser was using the wrong physical record mode.

Key `DecodeScenes` offsets:

| Native address | Instruction hex | Decoded instruction | Runtime meaning |
|---:|---|---|---|
| `0x00708c1e`-`0x00708c46` | `adds r7,r5,#2`; `bytesToShort(buf,r7)`; `adds r5,r7,#2` | first record in a logical subblock reads cmd at `current + 2` | This is the `u16 prefix`, `u16 cmd`, payload form. |
| `0x00708c66`-`0x00708c2a` | `adds r7,r5,#0`; loop back to `bytesToShort(buf,r7)` | open subblock reads cmd at the current offset | This is the cmd-only form. |
| `0x00708c60`-`0x00708c66` | `adds r5,r7,#4`; clear skip flag | `ScriptChildInfo` followed by raw zero can skip an extra short | Explains `R_01@0x002d` zero skip. |
| `0x00708dfc`-`0x00708e04` | `adds r5,#2`; optional append path resets mode variable | child/subscript mode may skip a short after a command | Explains choice/branch bytes such as `R_01@0x0888`. |

Concrete `R_01.eex_new` trace:

| Offset | Hex | Decode result | State |
|---:|---|---|---|
| `0x0020` | `72 00 02 00 05 00 e5 87 af e6 97 8b 00` | subblock-start record: prefix `0x0072`, cmd `0x0002 ScriptChildInfo`, text tag `0x0005`, UTF-8 `凯旋`; `initPara` returns `0x002d` | first record uses `prefix + cmd` |
| `0x002d` | `00 00 59 0a` | raw `cmd 0x0000` with child-info skip flag set; native skip path advances to `0x0031` | not a real end marker here |
| `0x0031` | `0a 00` | cmd-only `0x000a ScriptInitValue`; base `initPara` consumes no payload | open subblock command |
| `0x0033` | `2f 00` | cmd-only `0x002f ScriptClearActor`; no `initPara` override, so payload length `0` | open subblock command |
| `0x0035` | `08 00 2e 00 00 00` | cmd-only `0x0008 ScriptMenuVisible`; native `ScriptMenuVisible::initPara` consumes `4` bytes | two shorts |
| `0x003b` | `24 00 09 00 ff 00` | cmd-only `0x0024 ScriptMusicSet`; native `ScriptMusicSet::initPara` consumes `4` bytes | two shorts, not `DelaySet` under prefix mode |
| `0x00df` | `18 00 05 00 e5 87 af e6 97 8b 00` | cmd-only `0x0018 ScriptCommonInfo`, UTF-8 `凯旋` | scene title, not `prefix=0x0018/cmd=0x0005` |
| `0x00ea` | `17 00 05 00 e8 93 9f e5 9f 8e 20 20 e5 88 ba e5 8f b2 e5 ba 9c 00` | cmd-only `0x0017 ScriptCommonInfo`, UTF-8 `蓟城  刺史府` | scene location |
| `0x010a` | `14 00 05 00 26 e5 88 98 e7 84 89 0a ... 00` | cmd-only `0x0014 ScriptActorTalk`, UTF-8 dialogue beginning `&刘焉\n玄德果然不负我望。` | dialogue text is intact |
| `0x0866` | `12 00 05 00 e6 ac a3 ... e7 bb 9d 00 02 00 00 00` | cmd-only `0x0012 ScriptShowChoice`, option text `欣然接受\n婉言谢绝`, then two shorts | `initPara` returns `0x0888` |
| `0x0888` | `60 02 01 00` | after `ScriptShowChoice` returns `0x0888`, child/subscript skip consumes short `0x0260`; next command is `cmd 0x0001 Base1` at `0x088a` | begins first choice branch block |
| `0x088c` | `13 00 04 00 01 00 00 00` | cmd-only `0x0013 ScriptCase`; payload includes little-endian int `1` | first option branch for `欣然接受` |
| `0x0894` | `d2 00 3a 00 28 00 02 00 34 00 01 00 04 00 02 00` | after `ScriptCase` returns `0x0894`, child/subscript skip consumes short `0x00d2`; next command is `cmd 0x003a ScriptMoneyChange` at `0x0896` | first branch applies money reward path |
| `0x097a` | `69 00 05 00 e5 be 97 e5 88 b0 e4 ba 8c e5 8d 83 e9 92 b1 00` | cmd-only `0x0069 ScriptCommonInfo`, UTF-8 `得到二千钱` | reward text confirms branch effect |
| `0x0996` | `00 00 01 00 13 00 04 00 02 00 00 00` | cmd-only `0x0000 Base0` at `0x0996`, `0x0001 Base1` at `0x0998`, then `0x0013 ScriptCase` at `0x099a`; child/subscript skip consumes `0x0174` before `0x003a` at `0x09a4` | second option branch for `婉言谢绝` |

Length corrections and parser alignments from this trace:

| Command | Evidence | Correct parser action |
|---:|---|---|
| `0x0005 ScriptTestValue` | `ScriptTestValue::initPara@0x00709931` reads a leading short, count `n1`, then `n1` shorts, then another leading short, count `n2`, then `n2` shorts, and returns the advanced cursor. | Variable length: `4 + 2*n1 + 4 + 2*n2`; not fixed `12`. |
| `0x0004 ScriptTestAsk` | `R_01@0x0974` is followed by payload `01 00 00 00` and then valid `0x0069 ScriptCommonInfo` at `0x097a`; the section only reaches `0x0d5f` if `0x0004` consumes 4 bytes. | Fixed length `4` in the current parser model; native field labels still pending. |
| `0x0024 ScriptMusicSet` | `ScriptMusicSet::initPara@0x007131e9` reads two shorts and returns `payload + 4`. | Fixed length `4`. |
| `0x0023 ScriptSoundSet` | `ScriptSoundSet::initPara@0x00713139` reads three shorts, one int, and returns `payload + 0x0a`. | Fixed length `0x0a`; earlier `2`-byte assumptions desync R cutscene audio/action blocks. |
| `0x0025 ScriptTestActorPos` | `ScriptTestActorPos::initPara@0x007132f5` tail returns `payload + 0x10`. | Fixed length `0x10`; field semantics still partly named. |
| `0x0028 ScriptFreeMove` | `ScriptFreeMove::initPara@0x0071399d` reads two shorts and returns `payload + 4`. | Fixed length `4`. |
| `0x002b ScriptMapFaceDisAppear` | `ScriptMapFaceDisAppear::initPara@0x00713cdd` reads two shorts and returns `payload + 4`. | Fixed length `4`; earlier `2`-byte assumptions desync face/cutscene blocks. |
| `0x002f ScriptClearActor` | No `ScriptClearActor::initPara` override exists; only `saveScript`/handlers are present. | Base length `0`. |
| `0x0030 ScriptActorAppear` | `ScriptActorAppear::initPara@0x007146a5` reads through payload offset `+0x16` and returns `payload + 0x18`. | Fixed length `0x18`. |
| `0x0033 ScriptActorTurn` | `ScriptActorTurn::initPara@0x00714fd7` tail returns `payload + 0x0c`. | Fixed length `0x0c`; earlier `6`-byte assumptions desync repeated actor motion blocks. |
| `0x0034 ScriptActorAction` | `ScriptActorAction::initPara@0x00715089` reads four shorts and returns `payload + 8`; `R_01@0x013a`, `0x02f6`, `0x0362`, and later records align to following dialogue only with this length. | Fixed length `8`. |
| `0x003a ScriptMoneyChange` | `ScriptMoneyChange::initPara@0x0071667d` reads shorts at payload offsets `+0`, `+2`, `+4`, `+6`, `+8`, then an int at `+0x0a`, and returns `payload + 0x0e`. | Fixed length `0x0e`; earlier `0x0c` assumptions desync the choice reward branch. |
| `0x0037 ScriptMoneyTest` | `ScriptMoneyTest::initPara@0x00715e25` reads two shorts, one int, two more shorts, and returns `payload + 0x0e`. | Fixed length `0x0e`. |
| `0x003b ScriptArmyChange` | `ScriptArmyChange::initPara@0x00716eb1` reads six shorts and returns `payload + 0x0c`. | Fixed length `0x0c`. |
| `0x006b ScriptCallMagic` | `ScriptCallMagic::initPara@0x0070a831` tail returns `payload + 0x14`. | Fixed length `0x14`; field semantics not named. |
| `0x006d ScriptRelaReviveOrMove` | `ScriptRelaReviveOrMove::initPara@0x0070afb7` tail returns `payload + 0x26`. | Fixed length `0x26`; actor source, reference actor, offsets, direction, and move-vs-revive flag are decoded in section 4.8.2. Direction/list-source labels remain open. |
| `0x0072 ScriptMsgTransmit` | `ScriptMsgTransmit::initPara@0x0070c361` reads short at `+0`, int at `+2`, short at `+6`, then a DString at `payload + 8`; return is `payload + 8 + strlen0`. | Variable length `8 + NUL-terminated UTF-8 string`. |
| `0x0073 ScriptActorProperty` | `ScriptActorProperty::initPara@0x0070ea8f` tail returns `payload + 0x22`. | Fixed length `0x22`; field semantics not named. |
| `0x0078 ScriptValueIntValuation` | `ScriptValueIntValuation::initPara@0x0070fac7` reads one short, one int, then shorts through offset `+0x10`; tail returns `payload + 0x12`. | Fixed length `0x12`. |
| `0x002c ScriptMapTellInfo` | `ScriptMapTellInfo::initPara@0x00713e05` reads a short, a DString at `payload + 2`, then six shorts after the string; tail returns `stringEnd + 0x0c`. | Variable length `2 + strlen0 + 0x0c`. |
| `0x004d ScriptChangeActorState` | `ScriptChangeActorState::initPara@0x00719b35` tail returns `payload + 0x42`. | Fixed length `0x42`; source mode, direct/list/area targeting, side selector, op enum, status mask, HP delta, and MP delta are decoded in section 4.8.3. Human status labels remain open. |
| `0x0050 ScriptBattleActorAction` | `ScriptBattleActorAction::initPara@0x0071b705` tail returns `payload + 0x10`. | Fixed length `0x10`. |
| `0x0053 ScriptBattleActorLeave` | `ScriptBattleActorLeave::initPara@0x0071b973` tail returns `payload + 0x28`. | Fixed length `0x28`. |
| `0x0055 ScriptBattleActorRelive` | `ScriptBattleActorRelive::initPara@0x0071bde5` tail returns `payload + 0x1e`. | Fixed length `0x1e`; actor source, absolute x/y, and direction are decoded in section 4.8.2. Direction/list-source labels remain open. |
| `0x0058 ScriptSetBattleBarrier` | `ScriptSetBattleBarrier::initPara@0x0071c255` tail returns `payload + 0x20`. | Fixed length `0x20`; kind, add/remove flag, tile value, x/y, delay, and post-delay are decoded in section 4.8.5. Human element/tile labels remain open. |
| `0x0059 ScriptSetBattleBonus` | `ScriptSetBattleBonus::initPara@0x0071c3e3` tail returns `payload + 0x22`. | Fixed length `0x22`; money, three good-id slots, retained per-good extra fields, and tail field are decoded in section 4.8.6. Extra/tail labels remain open. |

After these corrections, plus the bulk native-length audit below, a temporary native-mode parser reaches the exact end of `R_01.eex_new` section `0x001e`:

```text
endstate rec 113 cur 0x0d5f end 0x0d5f remain 0
0x0864 cmd 0x0001 Base1 -> 0x0866
0x0866 cmd 0x0012 ShowChoice L=32 childskip=60 02 -> 0x088a
0x088a cmd 0x0001 Base1 -> 0x088c
0x088c cmd 0x0013 Case L=6 childskip=d2 00 -> 0x0896
0x0896 cmd 0x003a MoneyChange L=14 -> 0x08a6
0x0974 cmd 0x0004 TestAsk L=4 -> 0x097a
0x097a cmd 0x0069 CommonInfo L=18 -> 0x098e
0x0996 cmd 0x0000 Base0 -> 0x0998
0x0998 cmd 0x0001 Base1 -> 0x099a
0x099a cmd 0x0013 Case L=6 childskip=74 01 -> 0x09a4
0x0b77 cmd 0x003d GetGood L=16 -> 0x0b89
0x0b89/0x0b8b cmd 0x0000 Base0 -> 0x0b8d
0x0c09/0x0c29/0x0c49 cmd 0x0032 ActorMove L=30
0x0c69/0x0c8f/0x0cb5 cmd 0x0031 ActorDisappear L=36
0x0d5d cmd 0x0000 Base0 -> 0x0d5f
```

This is physical cursor evidence, not proof that the logical sublist reconstruction is solved.

### 4.12 Bulk Native `initPara` Audit

A temporary pyelftools/capstone pass over `libMyGame.so` found `100` `Script*::initPara` symbols and extracted fixed return shapes where the tail returns `payload + imm`. This replaced several earlier corpus-alignment guesses.

New native-proven corrections not already listed above:

| Command | Native evidence | Correct parser action |
|---:|---|---|
| `0x0006 ScriptForceLimit` | `ScriptForceLimit::initPara@0x00709ccd` reads fields through payload offset `+0x30`; tail returns `payload + 0x32`. | Fixed length `0x32`; not a zero-length structural marker. |
| `0x000b ScriptSetValue` | `ScriptSetValue::initPara@0x0070fa4d` tail returns `payload + 0x0a`. | Fixed length `0x0a`. |
| `0x000f ScriptGameEnding` | `ScriptGameEnding::initPara@0x00711225` returns `payload + 4`. | Fixed length `4`. |
| `0x0011 ScriptSceneChange` | `ScriptSceneChange::initPara@0x0071142b` returns `payload + 4`. | Fixed length `4`; this removes prior `unknown_len 0x11` failures. |

### 4.13 Superseded Corpus Probe Baseline

Temporary corpus scans were run over all `316` `Scenes/*.eex_new` files / `1608` sections after the bulk native length audit:

Status: superseded by the native-mode exact-end probe in section 4.14. This table is retained only as a baseline showing which failures were later explained by native `DecodeScenes` state, corrected dispatch child file lengths, and missing `initPara` lengths.

| Parser mode | Sections exact-end | Sections failed | Records parsed | Child skips | Notes |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---|
| native length table + bounded fallback: try cmd-only, then `prefix + cmd` when cmd-only fails | `1068` | `540` | `93049` | `4066` | Historical heuristic baseline; superseded by section 4.14. |
| extra heuristic: after `ScriptChildInfo`, prefer `prefix + cmd` when next short is nonzero | `948` | `660` | `62879` | `419` | Regressed coverage; not adopted as a rule. |

Top command counts in that superseded scan: `0x0009=18068`, `0x0014=11752`, `0x0034=9937`, `0x0000=7468`, `0x0030=4883`, `0x0033=4722`, `0x0001=4074`, `0x0032=3126`, `0x0002=2975`, `0x0077=2454`, `0x0024=1671`, `0x0079=1528`, `0x0023=1202`, `0x001d=1099`, `0x0027=1044`, `0x001c=1003`.

Representative old failures were parse-mode / field-length gaps:

| File | Section | Offset | Failure | Hex evidence | Interpretation |
|---|---:|---:|---|---|---|
| `R_00.eex_new` | `1` | `0x2864b` | `bad_cmd 0xe5a9` | `e7 8e a9 e5 ae b6 e5 88 87 e6 8d a2 00 ...` | Cursor landed inside UTF-8 `玩家切换`; section start bytes show `prefix=0x0005`, `cmd=0x0002 ScriptChildInfo`, then another `prefix=0x0005`, `cmd=0x0035`. Record-mode choice after `ScriptChildInfo` is still incomplete. |
| `R_01.eex_new` | `3` | `0x56be` | `bad_cmd 0xace6` | `05 00 e6 ac a1 e6 97 a5 e2 80 a6 e2 80 a6 00 ...` | Cursor landed inside UTF-8 `次日……`; still a length/mode miss. |
| `R_05.eex_new` | `0` | `0x0908` | `end_mismatch cur=0x908 end=0x906` | `72 00 02 00 05 00 e8 a2 81 e6 9c af ...` | Overran by two bytes; boundary/subblock close handling still off. |

Superseded interpretation: the failed greedy dumper was incomplete, not evidence of lost semantics. Section 4.14 replaces this baseline with a native-mode scan that reaches exact end for every section.

### 4.14 Exact-End Native-Mode Corpus Probe

The latest temporary probe uses the native `DecodeScenes` state model plus the corrected `Script*::initPara` lengths. It is still a read-only recon script, not a submitted converter.

| Parser mode | Files exact-end | Sections exact-end | Sections failed | Records parsed | Zero skips | Child skips | `ScriptChildInfo` records | Notes |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---|
| native `DecodeScenes` state + corrected child file lengths + `0x0026/0x0060/0x0063/0x0067` lengths | `316 / 316` | `1608 / 1608` | `0` | `1327396` | `9194` | `175400` | `28034` | Every section cursor reaches its header-declared end exactly. This proves physical byte structure is enumerable; it does not name every field enum. |

Top command counts in the exact-end scan: `0x0038=266953`, `0x0000=184580`, `0x0001=175400`, `0x0016=98499`, `0x000b=71834`, `0x0079=71381`, `0x0005=69361`, `0x0077=36998`, `0x0009=31066`, `0x0002=28034`, `0x0014=27720`, `0x0072=27001`, `0x0048=23905`, `0x0069=23263`, `0x006f=22066`, `0x0078=15054`, `0x0023=13858`, `0x0013=13505`, `0x0034=13172`, `0x003d=8474`, `0x0050=7639`, `0x004f=6535`, `0x0030=6130`, `0x0033=6041`, `0x0032=5551`, `0x004c=5486`, `0x0012=5404`, `0x003b=4072`.

Exact-end negative check for `0x005e`: a raw byte scan finds `311` `5e 00` occurrences in `101` `Scenes/*.eex_new` files, but the same exact-end walker records `0` occurrences where `5e 00` is a command offset. Representative false positives:

| File | Raw offset | Exact owner | Hex evidence | Decode result |
|---|---:|---|---|---|
| `R_01.eex_new` | `0x0db9` | `0x0030 ScriptActorAppear@0x0dab`, span `0x0dab..0x0dc5` | `30 00 02 00 01 00 04 00 2d 00 00 00 04 00 5e 00 00 00 2b 00 00 00 0d 00 00 00` | The `5e 00` word is inside an actor-appearance payload, not an opcode. |
| `R_02.eex_new` | `0x7936` | `0x0032 ScriptActorMove@0x791e`, span `0x791e..0x793e` | `32 00 40 00 ff ff 02 00 94 00 04 00 00 00 00 00 04 00 2c 00 00 00 04 00 5e 00 00 00 2b 00 02 00` | The `5e 00` word is a coordinate/value field in a move payload. |
| `R_03.eex_new` | `0x54e1` | `0x0030 ScriptActorAppear@0x54d3`, span `0x54d3..0x54ed` | `30 00 02 00 94 00 04 00 38 00 00 00 04 00 5e 00 00 00 2b 00 00 00 0d 00 00 00` | Another payload collision; exact cursor does not accept it as command `0x005e`. |

New closure evidence:

| File | Section | Offset | Hex evidence | Decode result |
|---|---:|---:|---|---|
| `S_00.eex_new` | `1` | `0x25672` | `60 00 26 00 00 00 05 00 e7 9c 8b e6 b1 9d e4 b8 80 e8 a1 a8 e4 ba ba e6 89 8d ef bc 8c ... 00 4c 00 06 00` | `0x0060 ScriptPKActorAppear`; fields `[0x0026, 0x0000, 0x0005]`; DString at payload `+6` decodes as Chinese PK dialogue; trailing shorts `[0x004c, 0x0006]`; cursor closes at `0x256f3`. |

| `S_00.eex_new` | `1` | `0x28aee` | `26 00 02 00 36 01 04 00 00 00 00 00 04 00 0b 00 00 00 04 00 01 00 00 00 04 00 0c 00 00 00` | `0x0026 ScriptTestActorArea`; fixed payload `0x1c`; words `[2, 310, 4, 0, 0, 4, 11, 0, 4, 1, 0, 4, 12, 0]`; area-condition structure is separable. |
